File Summary

Purpose:
--------
This file contains a packed representation of the entire repository's contents.
It is designed to be easily consumable by AI systems for analysis, code review,
or other automated processes.

File Format:
------------
The content is organized as follows:
1. This summary section
2. Repository information
3. Directory structure
4. Repository files (if enabled)
5. Multiple file entries, each consisting of:
  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)
  c. Another separator line
  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with
  the same level of security as you would the original repository.

Notes:
------
- Some files may have been excluded based on .gitignore rules and Repomix's configuration
- Binary files are not included in this packed representation. Please refer to the Repository Structure section for a complete list of file paths, including binary files
- Files matching patterns in .gitignore are excluded
- Files matching default ignore patterns are excluded
- Code comments have been removed from supported file types
- Empty lines have been removed from all files
- Line numbers have been added to the beginning of each line
- Content has been formatted for parsing in plain style
- Files are sorted by Git change count (files with more changes are at the bottom)

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/api-server/src/lib/business-info.ts
================
 1: import { promises as fs } from "node:fs";
 2: import path from "node:path";
 3: import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url";
 4: const here = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
 5: const DATA_FILE = path.resolve(here, "../data/business-info.json");
 6: export type BusinessInfo = {
 7:   businessName: string;
 8:   legalEntity: string;
 9:   city: string;
10:   primaryPhone: string;
11:   primaryPhoneRaw: string;
12:   primaryEmail: string;
13:   zellePhone: string;
14:   zellePhoneRaw: string;
15:   zelleEmail: string;
16:   venmoHandle: string;
17:   stripePaymentLink: string;
18:   calendarLink: string;
19:   instagramMain: string;
20:   instagramCloset: string;
21:   facebook: string;
22:   responseTime: string;
23: };
24: export async function readBusinessInfo(): Promise<BusinessInfo> {
25:   const raw = await fs.readFile(DATA_FILE, "utf8");
26:   return JSON.parse(raw) as BusinessInfo;
27: }
28: export async function writeBusinessInfo(next: BusinessInfo): Promise<void> {
29:   const current = await readBusinessInfo();
30:   const merged: BusinessInfo = { ...current, ...next };
31:   await fs.writeFile(DATA_FILE, JSON.stringify(merged, null, 2) + "\n", "utf8");
32: }

 1: import pino from "pino";
 2: const isProduction = process.env.NODE_ENV === "production";
 3: export const logger = pino({
 4:   level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL ?? "info",
 5:   redact: [
 6:     "req.headers.authorization",
 7:     "req.headers.cookie",
 8:     "res.headers['set-cookie']",
 9:   ],
10:   ...(isProduction
11:     ? {}
12:     : {
13:         transport: {
14:           target: "pino-pretty",
15:           options: { colorize: true },
16:         },
17:       }),
18: });

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/api-server/src/routes/business-info.ts
================
 1: import { Router, type IRouter } from "express";
 2: import { readBusinessInfo, writeBusinessInfo } from "../lib/business-info";
 3: const router: IRouter = Router();
 4: router.get("/business-info", async (_req, res) => {
 5:   try {
 6:     const info = await readBusinessInfo();
 7:     res.json(info);
 8:   } catch (err) {
 9:     res.status(500).json({ error: "Could not load business info." });
10:   }
11: });
12: router.put("/business-info", async (req, res) => {
13:   const expected = process.env.ADMIN_PASSWORD;
14:   if (!expected) {
15:     res.status(503).json({
16:       error:
17:         "Admin editing is disabled. Set the ADMIN_PASSWORD secret to enable saving.",
18:     });
19:     return;
20:   }
21:   const provided = req.header("x-admin-password");
22:   if (provided !== expected) {
23:     res.status(401).json({ error: "Wrong password." });
24:     return;
25:   }
26:   try {
27:     await writeBusinessInfo(req.body);
28:     const info = await readBusinessInfo();
29:     res.json(info);
30:   } catch (err) {
31:     res.status(500).json({ error: "Could not save business info." });
32:   }
33: });
34: export default router;

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/api-server/src/app.ts
================
 1: import express, { type Express } from "express";
 2: import cors from "cors";
 3: import pinoHttp from "pino-http";
 4: import router from "./routes";
 5: import { logger } from "./lib/logger";
 6: const app: Express = express();
 7: app.use(
 8:   pinoHttp({
 9:     logger,
10:     serializers: {
11:       req(req) {
12:         return {
13:           id: req.id,
14:           method: req.method,
15:           url: req.url?.split("?")[0],
16:         };
17:       },
18:       res(res) {
19:         return {
20:           statusCode: res.statusCode,
21:         };
22:       },
23:     },
24:   }),
25: );
26: app.use(cors());
27: app.use(express.json());
28: app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
29: app.use("/api", router);
30: export default app;

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/api-server/src/index.ts
================
 1: import app from "./app";
 2: import { logger } from "./lib/logger";
 3: const rawPort = process.env["PORT"];
 4: if (!rawPort) {
 5:   throw new Error(
 6:     "PORT environment variable is required but was not provided.",
 7:   );
 8: }
 9: const port = Number(rawPort);
10: if (Number.isNaN(port) || port <= 0) {
11:   throw new Error(`Invalid PORT value: "${rawPort}"`);
12: }
13: app.listen(port, (err) => {
14:   if (err) {
15:     logger.error({ err }, "Error listening on port");
16:     process.exit(1);
17:   }
18:   logger.info({ port }, "Server listening");
19: });

 2: import * as AccordionPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-accordion"
 3: import { ChevronDown } from "lucide-react"
 4: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
 5: const Accordion = AccordionPrimitive.Root
 6: const AccordionItem = React.forwardRef<
 7:   React.ElementRef<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Item>,

 1: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"

 5: const buttonGroupVariants = cva(
 6:   "flex w-fit items-stretch has-[>[data-slot=button-group]]:gap-2 [&>*]:focus-visible:relative [&>*]:focus-visible:z-10 has-[select[aria-hidden=true]:last-child]:[&>[data-slot=select-trigger]:last-of-type]:rounded-r-md [&>[data-slot=select-trigger]:not([class*='w-'])]:w-fit [&>input]:flex-1",
 7:   {
 8:     variants: {
 9:       orientation: {
10:         horizontal:
11:           "[&>*:not(:first-child)]:rounded-l-none [&>*:not(:first-child)]:border-l-0 [&>*:not(:last-child)]:rounded-r-none",
12:         vertical:
13:           "flex-col [&>*:not(:first-child)]:rounded-t-none [&>*:not(:first-child)]:border-t-0 [&>*:not(:last-child)]:rounded-b-none",

19:   }

39:   ...props

48:         className
49:       )}
50:       {...props}
51:     />
52:   )
53: }

58: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Separator>) {

  1: import * as React from "react"
  2: import useEmblaCarousel, {
  3:   type UseEmblaCarouselType,
  4: } from "embla-carousel-react"
  5: import { ArrowLeft, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react"
  6: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
  7: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"
  8: type CarouselApi = UseEmblaCarouselType[1]
  9: type UseCarouselParameters = Parameters<typeof useEmblaCarousel>
 10: type CarouselOptions = UseCarouselParameters[0]
 11: type CarouselPlugin = UseCarouselParameters[1]
 12: type CarouselProps = {
 13:   opts?: CarouselOptions
 14:   plugins?: CarouselPlugin
 15:   orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical"
 16:   setApi?: (api: CarouselApi) => void
 17: }
 18: type CarouselContextProps = {
 19:   carouselRef: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[0]
 20:   api: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[1]
 21:   scrollPrev: () => void
 22:   scrollNext: () => void
 23:   canScrollPrev: boolean
 24:   canScrollNext: boolean
 25: } & CarouselProps
 26: const CarouselContext = React.createContext<CarouselContextProps | null>(null)
 27: function useCarousel() {
 28:   const context = React.useContext(CarouselContext)
 29:   if (!context) {
 30:     throw new Error("useCarousel must be used within a <Carousel />")
 31:   }
 32:   return context
 33: }
 34: const Carousel = React.forwardRef<
 35:   HTMLDivElement,
 36:   React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> & CarouselProps
 37: >(
 38:   (
 39:     {
 40:       orientation = "horizontal",
 41:       opts,
 42:       setApi,
 43:       plugins,
 44:       className,
 45:       children,
 46:       ...props
 47:     },
 48:     ref
 49:   ) => {
 50:     const [carouselRef, api] = useEmblaCarousel(
 51:       {
 52:         ...opts,
 53:         axis: orientation === "horizontal" ? "x" : "y",
 54:       },
 55:       plugins
 56:     )
 57:     const [canScrollPrev, setCanScrollPrev] = React.useState(false)
 58:     const [canScrollNext, setCanScrollNext] = React.useState(false)
 59:     const onSelect = React.useCallback((api: CarouselApi) => {
 60:       if (!api) {
 61:         return
 62:       }
 63:       setCanScrollPrev(api.canScrollPrev())
 64:       setCanScrollNext(api.canScrollNext())
 65:     }, [])
 66:     const scrollPrev = React.useCallback(() => {
 67:       api?.scrollPrev()
 68:     }, [api])
 69:     const scrollNext = React.useCallback(() => {
 70:       api?.scrollNext()
 71:     }, [api])
 72:     const handleKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 73:       (event: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
 74:         if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
 75:           event.preventDefault()
 76:           scrollPrev()
 77:         } else if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
 78:           event.preventDefault()
 79:           scrollNext()
 80:         }
 81:       },
 82:       [scrollPrev, scrollNext]
 83:     )
 84:     React.useEffect(() => {
 85:       if (!api || !setApi) {
 86:         return
 87:       }
 88:       setApi(api)
 89:     }, [api, setApi])
 90:     React.useEffect(() => {
 91:       if (!api) {
 92:         return
 93:       }
 94:       onSelect(api)
 95:       api.on("reInit", onSelect)
 96:       api.on("select", onSelect)
 97:       return () => {
 98:         api?.off("select", onSelect)
 99:       }
100:     }, [api, onSelect])
101:     return (
102:       <CarouselContext.Provider
103:         value={{
104:           carouselRef,
105:           api: api,
106:           opts,
107:           orientation:
108:             orientation || (opts?.axis === "y" ? "vertical" : "horizontal"),
109:           scrollPrev,
110:           scrollNext,
111:           canScrollPrev,
112:           canScrollNext,
113:         }}
114:       >
115:         <div
116:           ref={ref}
117:           onKeyDownCapture={handleKeyDown}
118:           className={cn("relative", className)}
119:           role="region"
120:           aria-roledescription="carousel"
121:           {...props}
122:         >
123:           {children}
124:         </div>
125:       </CarouselContext.Provider>
126:     )
127:   }
128: )
129: Carousel.displayName = "Carousel"
130: const CarouselContent = React.forwardRef<
131:   HTMLDivElement,
132:   React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>
133: >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => {
134:   const { carouselRef, orientation } = useCarousel()
135:   return (
136:     <div ref={carouselRef} className="overflow-hidden">
137:       <div
138:         ref={ref}
139:         className={cn(
140:           "flex",
141:           orientation === "horizontal" ? "-ml-4" : "-mt-4 flex-col",
142:           className
143:         )}
144:         {...props}
145:       />
146:     </div>
147:   )
148: })

190:                                 "w-0 border-[1.5px] border-dashed bg-transparent":
191:                                   indicator === "dashed",
192:                                 "my-0.5": nestLabel && indicator === "dashed",
193:                               }
194:                             )}
195:                             style={
196:                               {
197:                                 "--color-bg": indicatorColor,
198:                                 "--color-border": indicatorColor,
199:                               } as React.CSSProperties
200:                             }
201:                           />
202:                         )
203:                       )}
204:                       <div
205:                         className={cn(
206:                           "flex flex-1 justify-between leading-none",
207:                           nestLabel ? "items-end" : "items-center"
208:                         )}
209:                       >
210:                         <div className="grid gap-1.5">
211:                           {nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
212:                           <span className="text-muted-foreground">
213:                             {itemConfig?.label || item.name}
214:                           </span>
215:                         </div>
216:                         {item.value && (
217:                           <span className="font-mono font-medium tabular-nums text-foreground">
218:                             {item.value.toLocaleString()}
219:                           </span>
220:                         )}
221:                       </div>
222:                     </>
223:                   )}
224:                 </div>
225:               )
226:             })}
227:         </div>
228:       </div>
229:     )
230:   }
231: )
232: ChartTooltipContent.displayName = "ChartTooltip"
233: const ChartLegend = RechartsPrimitive.Legend
234: const ChartLegendContent = React.forwardRef<
235:   HTMLDivElement,
236:   React.ComponentProps<"div"> &
237:     Pick<RechartsPrimitive.LegendProps, "payload" | "verticalAlign"> & {
238:       hideIcon?: boolean
239:       nameKey?: string
240:     }
241: >(
242:   (
243:     { className, hideIcon = false, payload, verticalAlign = "bottom", nameKey },
244:     ref
245:   ) => {
246:     const { config } = useChart()
247:     if (!payload?.length) {
248:       return null
249:     }
250:     return (
251:       <div
252:         ref={ref}
253:         className={cn(
254:           "flex items-center justify-center gap-4",
255:           verticalAlign === "top" ? "pb-3" : "pt-3",
256:           className
257:         )}
258:       >
259:         {payload
260:           .filter((item) => item.type !== "none")
261:           .map((item) => {
262:             const key = `${nameKey || item.dataKey || "value"}`
263:             const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key)
264:             return (
265:               <div
266:                 key={item.value}
267:                 className={cn(
268:                   "flex items-center gap-1.5 [&>svg]:h-3 [&>svg]:w-3 [&>svg]:text-muted-foreground"
269:                 )}
270:               >
271:                 {itemConfig?.icon && !hideIcon ? (
272:                   <itemConfig.icon />
273:                 ) : (
274:                   <div
275:                     className="h-2 w-2 shrink-0 rounded-[2px]"
276:                     style={{
277:                       backgroundColor: item.color,
278:                     }}
279:                   />
280:                 )}
281:                 {itemConfig?.label}
282:               </div>
283:             )
284:           })}
285:       </div>
286:     )
287:   }
288: )
289: ChartLegendContent.displayName = "ChartLegend"
290: function getPayloadConfigFromPayload(
291:   config: ChartConfig,
292:   payload: unknown,
293:   key: string
294: ) {
295:   if (typeof payload !== "object" || payload === null) {
296:     return undefined
297:   }
298:   const payloadPayload =
299:     "payload" in payload &&
300:     typeof payload.payload === "object" &&
301:     payload.payload !== null
302:       ? payload.payload
303:       : undefined
304:   let configLabelKey: string = key
305:   if (
306:     key in payload &&
307:     typeof payload[key as keyof typeof payload] === "string"
308:   ) {
309:     configLabelKey = payload[key as keyof typeof payload] as string
310:   } else if (
311:     payloadPayload &&
312:     key in payloadPayload &&
313:     typeof payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] === "string"
314:   ) {
315:     configLabelKey = payloadPayload[
316:       key as keyof typeof payloadPayload
317:     ] as string
318:   }
319:   return configLabelKey in config
320:     ? config[configLabelKey]
321:     : config[key as keyof typeof config]
322: }
323: export {
324:   ChartContainer,
325:   ChartTooltip,
326:   ChartTooltipContent,
327:   ChartLegend,
328:   ChartLegendContent,
329:   ChartStyle,
330: }

173: function FieldError({
174:   className,
175:   children,
176:   errors,
177:   ...props
178: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
179:   errors?: Array<{ message?: string } | undefined>
180: }) {
181:   const content = useMemo(() => {
182:     if (children) {
183:       return children
184:     }
185:     if (!errors) {
186:       return null
187:     }
188:     if (errors?.length === 1 && errors[0]?.message) {
189:       return errors[0].message
190:     }
191:     return (
192:       <ul className="ml-4 flex list-disc flex-col gap-1">
193:         {errors.map(
194:           (error, index) =>
195:             error?.message && <li key={index}>{error.message}</li>
196:         )}
197:       </ul>
198:     )
199:   }, [children, errors])
200:   if (!content) {
201:     return null
202:   }
203:   return (
204:     <div
205:       role="alert"
206:       data-slot="field-error"
207:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm font-normal", className)}
208:       {...props}
209:     >
210:       {content}
211:     </div>
212:   )
213: }
214: export {
215:   Field,
216:   FieldLabel,
217:   FieldDescription,
218:   FieldError,
219:   FieldGroup,
220:   FieldLegend,
221:   FieldSeparator,
222:   FieldSet,
223:   FieldContent,
224:   FieldTitle,
225: }

  1: import * as React from "react"
  2: import * as LabelPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-label"
  3: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
  4: import {
  5:   Controller,
  6:   FormProvider,
  7:   useFormContext,
  8:   type ControllerProps,
  9:   type FieldPath,
 10:   type FieldValues,
 11: } from "react-hook-form"
 12: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
 13: import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label"
 14: const Form = FormProvider
 15: type FormFieldContextValue<
 16:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 17:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>
 18: > = {
 19:   name: TName
 20: }
 21: const FormFieldContext = React.createContext<FormFieldContextValue | null>(null)
 22: const FormField = <
 23:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 24:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>
 25: >({
 26:   ...props
 27: }: ControllerProps<TFieldValues, TName>) => {
 28:   return (
 29:     <FormFieldContext.Provider value={{ name: props.name }}>
 30:       <Controller {...props} />
 31:     </FormFieldContext.Provider>
 32:   )
 33: }
 34: const useFormField = () => {
 35:   const fieldContext = React.useContext(FormFieldContext)
 36:   const itemContext = React.useContext(FormItemContext)
 37:   const { getFieldState, formState } = useFormContext()
 38:   if (!fieldContext) {
 39:     throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormField>")
 40:   }
 41:   if (!itemContext) {
 42:     throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormItem>")
 43:   }
 44:   const fieldState = getFieldState(fieldContext.name, formState)
 45:   const { id } = itemContext
 46:   return {
 47:     id,
 48:     name: fieldContext.name,
 49:     formItemId: `${id}-form-item`,
 50:     formDescriptionId: `${id}-form-item-description`,
 51:     formMessageId: `${id}-form-item-message`,
 52:     ...fieldState,
 53:   }
 54: }
 55: type FormItemContextValue = {
 56:   id: string
 57: }
 58: const FormItemContext = React.createContext<FormItemContextValue | null>(null)
 59: const FormItem = React.forwardRef<
 60:   HTMLDivElement,
 61:   React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>
 62: >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => {
 63:   const id = React.useId()
 64:   return (
 65:     <FormItemContext.Provider value={{ id }}>
 66:       <div ref={ref} className={cn("space-y-2", className)} {...props} />
 67:     </FormItemContext.Provider>
 68:   )
 69: })
 70: FormItem.displayName = "FormItem"
 71: const FormLabel = React.forwardRef<
 72:   React.ElementRef<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>,
 73:   React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>
 74: >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => {
 75:   const { error, formItemId } = useFormField()
 76:   return (
 77:     <Label
 78:       ref={ref}
 79:       className={cn(error && "text-destructive", className)}
 80:       htmlFor={formItemId}
 81:       {...props}
 82:     />
 83:   )
 84: })
 85: FormLabel.displayName = "FormLabel"
 86: const FormControl = React.forwardRef<
 87:   React.ElementRef<typeof Slot>,
 88:   React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof Slot>
 89: >(({ ...props }, ref) => {
 90:   const { error, formItemId, formDescriptionId, formMessageId } = useFormField()
 91:   return (
 92:     <Slot
 93:       ref={ref}
 94:       id={formItemId}
 95:       aria-describedby={
 96:         !error
 97:           ? `${formDescriptionId}`
 98:           : `${formDescriptionId} ${formMessageId}`
 99:       }
100:       aria-invalid={!!error}
101:       {...props}
102:     />
103:   )
104: })
105: FormControl.displayName = "FormControl"
106: const FormDescription = React.forwardRef<

117:     />
118:   )
119: })
120: FormDescription.displayName = "FormDescription"

129:   }
130:   return (

138:     </p>

140: })
141: FormMessage.displayName = "FormMessage"

  7: const Sheet = SheetPrimitive.Root
  8: const SheetTrigger = SheetPrimitive.Trigger
  9: const SheetClose = SheetPrimitive.Close

 11: const SheetOverlay = React.forwardRef<
 12:   React.ElementRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Overlay>,
 13:   React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Overlay>
 14: >(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
 15:   <SheetPrimitive.Overlay
 16:     className={cn(
 17:       "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80  data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
 18:       className
 19:     )}
 20:     {...props}
 21:     ref={ref}
 22:   />
 23: ))

 26:   "fixed z-50 gap-4 bg-background p-6 shadow-lg transition ease-in-out data-[state=closed]:duration-300 data-[state=open]:duration-500 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out",
 27:   {
 28:     variants: {
 29:       side: {
 30:         top: "inset-x-0 top-0 border-b data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top",

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/mockup-sandbox/src/components/ui/sidebar.tsx
================
  1: "use client"
  2: import * as React from "react"
  3: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
  4: import { cva, VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"
  5: import { PanelLeftIcon } from "lucide-react"
  6: import { useIsMobile } from "@/hooks/use-mobile"
  7: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
  8: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"
  9: import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input"
 10: import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator"
 11: import {
 12:   Sheet,
 13:   SheetContent,
 14:   SheetDescription,
 15:   SheetHeader,
 16:   SheetTitle,
 17: } from "@/components/ui/sheet"
 18: import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton"
 19: import {
 20:   Tooltip,
 21:   TooltipContent,
 22:   TooltipProvider,
 23:   TooltipTrigger,
 24: } from "@/components/ui/tooltip"
 25: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME = "sidebar_state"
 26: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE = 60 * 60 * 24 * 7
 27: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH = "16rem"
 28: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE = "18rem"
 29: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON = "3rem"
 30: const SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT = "b"
 31: type SidebarContextProps = {
 32:   state: "expanded" | "collapsed"
 33:   open: boolean
 34:   setOpen: (open: boolean) => void
 35:   openMobile: boolean
 36:   setOpenMobile: (open: boolean) => void
 37:   isMobile: boolean
 38:   toggleSidebar: () => void
 39: }
 40: const SidebarContext = React.createContext<SidebarContextProps | null>(null)
 41: function useSidebar() {
 42:   const context = React.useContext(SidebarContext)
 43:   if (!context) {
 44:     throw new Error("useSidebar must be used within a SidebarProvider.")
 45:   }
 46:   return context
 47: }
 48: function SidebarProvider({
 49:   defaultOpen = true,
 50:   open: openProp,
 51:   onOpenChange: setOpenProp,
 52:   className,
 53:   style,
 54:   children,
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
 57:   defaultOpen?: boolean
 58:   open?: boolean
 59:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void
 60: }) {
 61:   const isMobile = useIsMobile()
 62:   const [openMobile, setOpenMobile] = React.useState(false)
 63:   const [_open, _setOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen)
 64:   const open = openProp ?? _open
 65:   const setOpen = React.useCallback(
 66:     (value: boolean | ((value: boolean) => boolean)) => {
 67:       const openState = typeof value === "function" ? value(open) : value
 68:       if (setOpenProp) {
 69:         setOpenProp(openState)
 70:       } else {
 71:         _setOpen(openState)
 72:       }
 73:       document.cookie = `${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME}=${openState}; path=/; max-age=${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE}`
 74:     },
 75:     [setOpenProp, open]
 76:   )
 77:   const toggleSidebar = React.useCallback(() => {
 78:     return isMobile ? setOpenMobile((open) => !open) : setOpen((open) => !open)
 79:   }, [isMobile, setOpen, setOpenMobile])
 80:   React.useEffect(() => {
 81:     const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
 82:       if (
 83:         event.key === SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT &&
 84:         (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)
 85:       ) {
 86:         event.preventDefault()
 87:         toggleSidebar()
 88:       }
 89:     }
 90:     window.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown)
 91:     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown)
 92:   }, [toggleSidebar])
 93:   const state = open ? "expanded" : "collapsed"
 94:   const contextValue = React.useMemo<SidebarContextProps>(
 95:     () => ({
 96:       state,
 97:       open,
 98:       setOpen,
 99:       isMobile,
100:       openMobile,
101:       setOpenMobile,
102:       toggleSidebar,
103:     }),
104:     [state, open, setOpen, isMobile, openMobile, setOpenMobile, toggleSidebar]
105:   )
106:   return (
107:     <SidebarContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
108:       <TooltipProvider delayDuration={0}>
109:         <div
110:           data-slot="sidebar-wrapper"
111:           style={
112:             {
113:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH,
114:               "--sidebar-width-icon": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON,
115:               ...style,
116:             } as React.CSSProperties
117:           }
118:           className={cn(
119:             "group/sidebar-wrapper has-data-[variant=inset]:bg-sidebar flex min-h-svh w-full",
120:             className
121:           )}
122:           {...props}
123:         >
124:           {children}
125:         </div>
126:       </TooltipProvider>
127:     </SidebarContext.Provider>
128:   )
129: }
130: function Sidebar({
131:   side = "left",
132:   variant = "sidebar",
133:   collapsible = "offcanvas",
134:   className,
135:   children,
136:   ...props
137: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
138:   side?: "left" | "right"
139:   variant?: "sidebar" | "floating" | "inset"
140:   collapsible?: "offcanvas" | "icon" | "none"
141: }) {
142:   const { isMobile, state, openMobile, setOpenMobile } = useSidebar()
143:   if (collapsible === "none") {
144:     return (
145:       <div
146:         data-slot="sidebar"
147:         className={cn(
148:           "bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground flex h-full w-[var(--sidebar-width)] flex-col",
149:           className
150:         )}
151:         {...props}
152:       >
153:         {children}
154:       </div>
155:     )
156:   }
157:   if (isMobile) {
158:     return (
159:       <Sheet open={openMobile} onOpenChange={setOpenMobile} {...props}>
160:         <SheetContent
161:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
162:           data-slot="sidebar"
163:           data-mobile="true"
164:           className="bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground w-[var(--sidebar-width)] p-0 [&>button]:hidden"
165:           style={
166:             {
167:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE,
168:             } as React.CSSProperties
169:           }
170:           side={side}
171:         >
172:           <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
173:             <SheetTitle>Sidebar</SheetTitle>
174:             <SheetDescription>Displays the mobile sidebar.</SheetDescription>
175:           </SheetHeader>
176:           <div className="flex h-full w-full flex-col">{children}</div>
177:         </SheetContent>
178:       </Sheet>
179:     )
180:   }
181:   return (
182:     <div
183:       className="group peer text-sidebar-foreground hidden md:block"
184:       data-state={state}
185:       data-collapsible={state === "collapsed" ? collapsible : ""}
186:       data-variant={variant}
187:       data-side={side}
188:       data-slot="sidebar"
189:     >
190:       <div
191:         data-slot="sidebar-gap"
192:         className={cn(
193:           "relative w-[var(--sidebar-width)] bg-transparent transition-[width] duration-200 ease-linear",
194:           "group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:w-0",
195:           "group-data-[side=right]:rotate-180",
196:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
197:             ? "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+var(--spacing-4))]"
198:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[var(--sidebar-width-icon)]"
199:         )}
200:       />
201:       <div
202:         data-slot="sidebar-container"
203:         className={cn(
204:           "fixed inset-y-0 z-10 hidden h-svh w-[var(--sidebar-width)] transition-[left,right,width] duration-200 ease-linear md:flex",
205:           side === "left"
206:             ? "left-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:left-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]"
207:             : "right-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:right-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]",
208:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
209:             ? "p-2 group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+var(--spacing-4)+2px)]"
210:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[var(--sidebar-width-icon)] group-data-[side=left]:border-r group-data-[side=right]:border-l",
211:           className
212:         )}
213:         {...props}
214:       >
215:         <div
216:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
217:           data-slot="sidebar-inner"
218:           className="bg-sidebar group-data-[variant=floating]:border-sidebar-border flex h-full w-full flex-col group-data-[variant=floating]:rounded-lg group-data-[variant=floating]:border group-data-[variant=floating]:shadow-sm"
219:         >
220:           {children}
221:         </div>
222:       </div>
223:     </div>
224:   )
225: }

448: function SidebarMenuButton({
449:   asChild = false,
450:   isActive = false,
451:   variant = "default",
452:   size = "default",
453:   tooltip,
454:   className,
455:   ...props
456: }: React.ComponentProps<"button"> & {
457:   asChild?: boolean
458:   isActive?: boolean
459:   tooltip?: string | React.ComponentProps<typeof TooltipContent>
460: } & VariantProps<typeof sidebarMenuButtonVariants>) {
461:   const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"
462:   const { isMobile, state } = useSidebar()
463:   const button = (
464:     <Comp
465:       data-slot="sidebar-menu-button"
466:       data-sidebar="menu-button"
467:       data-size={size}
468:       data-active={isActive}
469:       className={cn(sidebarMenuButtonVariants({ variant, size }), className)}

471:     />
472:   )
473:   if (!tooltip) {
474:     return button
475:   }

477:     tooltip = {
478:       children: tooltip,
479:     }

481:   return (
482:     <Tooltip>

484:       <TooltipContent
485:         side="right"
486:         align="center"
487:         hidden={state !== "collapsed" || isMobile}
488:         {...tooltip}
489:       />
490:     </Tooltip>
491:   )
492: }

 2: import {
 3:   Toast,
 4:   ToastClose,
 5:   ToastDescription,
 6:   ToastProvider,
 7:   ToastTitle,
 8:   ToastViewport,
 9: } from "@/components/ui/toast"

12:   return (
13:     <ToastProvider>
14:       {toasts.map(function ({ id, title, description, action, ...props }) {
15:         return (

18:               {title && <ToastTitle>{title}</ToastTitle>}

20:                 <ToastDescription>{description}</ToastDescription>
21:               )}
22:             </div>
23:             {action}
24:             <ToastClose />
25:           </Toast>
26:         )
27:       })}
28:       <ToastViewport />
29:     </ToastProvider>
30:   )

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/mockup-sandbox/src/hooks/use-mobile.tsx
================
 1: import * as React from "react"
 2: const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768
 3: export function useIsMobile() {
 4:   const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined)
 5:   React.useEffect(() => {
 6:     const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`)
 7:     const onChange = () => {
 8:       setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
 9:     }
10:     mql.addEventListener("change", onChange)
11:     setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
12:     return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange)
13:   }, [])
14:   return !!isMobile
15: }

================
File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/mockup-sandbox/src/hooks/use-toast.ts
================
  1: import * as React from "react"
  2: import type {
  3:   ToastActionElement,
  4:   ToastProps,
  5: } from "@/components/ui/toast"
  6: const TOAST_LIMIT = 1
  7: const TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY = 1000000
  8: type ToasterToast = ToastProps & {
  9:   id: string
 10:   title?: React.ReactNode
 11:   description?: React.ReactNode
 12:   action?: ToastActionElement
 13: }
 14: const actionTypes = {
 15:   ADD_TOAST: "ADD_TOAST",
 16:   UPDATE_TOAST: "UPDATE_TOAST",
 17:   DISMISS_TOAST: "DISMISS_TOAST",
 18:   REMOVE_TOAST: "REMOVE_TOAST",
 19: } as const
 20: let count = 0
 21: function genId() {
 22:   count = (count + 1) % Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER
 23:   return count.toString()
 24: }
 25: type ActionType = typeof actionTypes
 26: type Action =
 27:   | {
 28:       type: ActionType["ADD_TOAST"]
 29:       toast: ToasterToast
 30:     }
 31:   | {
 32:       type: ActionType["UPDATE_TOAST"]
 33:       toast: Partial<ToasterToast>
 34:     }
 35:   | {
 36:       type: ActionType["DISMISS_TOAST"]
 37:       toastId?: ToasterToast["id"]
 38:     }
 39:   | {
 40:       type: ActionType["REMOVE_TOAST"]
 41:       toastId?: ToasterToast["id"]
 42:     }
 43: interface State {
 44:   toasts: ToasterToast[]
 45: }
 46: const toastTimeouts = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>()
 47: const addToRemoveQueue = (toastId: string) => {
 48:   if (toastTimeouts.has(toastId)) {
 49:     return
 50:   }
 51:   const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
 52:     toastTimeouts.delete(toastId)
 53:     dispatch({
 54:       type: "REMOVE_TOAST",
 55:       toastId: toastId,
 56:     })
 57:   }, TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY)
 58:   toastTimeouts.set(toastId, timeout)
 59: }
 60: export const reducer = (state: State, action: Action): State => {
 61:   switch (action.type) {
 62:     case "ADD_TOAST":
 63:       return {
 64:         ...state,
 65:         toasts: [action.toast, ...state.toasts].slice(0, TOAST_LIMIT),
 66:       }
 67:     case "UPDATE_TOAST":
 68:       return {
 69:         ...state,
 70:         toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
 71:           t.id === action.toast.id ? { ...t, ...action.toast } : t
 72:         ),
 73:       }
 74:     case "DISMISS_TOAST": {
 75:       const { toastId } = action
 76:       if (toastId) {
 77:         addToRemoveQueue(toastId)
 78:       } else {
 79:         state.toasts.forEach((toast) => {
 80:           addToRemoveQueue(toast.id)
 81:         })
 82:       }
 83:       return {
 84:         ...state,
 85:         toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>
 86:           t.id === toastId || toastId === undefined
 87:             ? {
 88:                 ...t,
 89:                 open: false,
 90:               }
 91:             : t
 92:         ),
 93:       }
 94:     }
 95:     case "REMOVE_TOAST":
 96:       if (action.toastId === undefined) {
 97:         return {
 98:           ...state,
 99:           toasts: [],
100:         }
101:       }
102:       return {
103:         ...state,
104:         toasts: state.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.toastId),
105:       }
106:   }
107: }
108: const listeners: Array<(state: State) => void> = []
109: let memoryState: State = { toasts: [] }
110: function dispatch(action: Action) {
111:   memoryState = reducer(memoryState, action)
112:   listeners.forEach((listener) => {
113:     listener(memoryState)
114:   })
115: }
116: type Toast = Omit<ToasterToast, "id">
117: function toast({ ...props }: Toast) {
118:   const id = genId()
119:   const update = (props: ToasterToast) =>
120:     dispatch({
121:       type: "UPDATE_TOAST",
122:       toast: { ...props, id },
123:     })
124:   const dismiss = () => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId: id })
125:   dispatch({
126:     type: "ADD_TOAST",
127:     toast: {
128:       ...props,
129:       id,
130:       open: true,
131:       onOpenChange: (open) => {
132:         if (!open) dismiss()
133:       },
134:     },
135:   })
136:   return {
137:     id: id,
138:     dismiss,
139:     update,
140:   }
141: }
142: function useToast() {
143:   const [state, setState] = React.useState<State>(memoryState)
144:   React.useEffect(() => {
145:     listeners.push(setState)
146:     return () => {
147:       const index = listeners.indexOf(setState)
148:       if (index > -1) {
149:         listeners.splice(index, 1)
150:       }
151:     }
152:   }, [state])
153:   return {
154:     ...state,
155:     toast,
156:     dismiss: (toastId?: string) => dispatch({ type: "DISMISS_TOAST", toastId }),
157:   }
158: }
159: export { useToast, toast }

File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/mockup-sandbox/src/App.tsx

  1: import { useEffect, useState, type ComponentType } from "react";
  2: import { modules as discoveredModules } from "./.generated/mockup-components";
  3: type ModuleMap = Record<string, () => Promise<Record<string, unknown>>>;
  4: function _resolveComponent(
  5:   mod: Record<string, unknown>,
  6:   name: string,
  7: ): ComponentType | undefined {
  8:   const fns = Object.values(mod).filter(
  9:     (v) => typeof v === "function",
 10:   ) as ComponentType[];
 11:   return (
 12:     (mod.default as ComponentType) ||
 13:     (mod.Preview as ComponentType) ||
 14:     (mod[name] as ComponentType) ||
 15:     fns[fns.length - 1]
 16:   );
 17: }
 18: function PreviewRenderer({
 19:   componentPath,
 20:   modules,
 21: }: {
 22:   componentPath: string;
 23:   modules: ModuleMap;
 24: }) {
 25:   const [Component, setComponent] = useState<ComponentType | null>(null);
 26:   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
 27:   useEffect(() => {
 28:     let cancelled = false;
 29:     setComponent(null);
 30:     setError(null);
 31:     async function loadComponent(): Promise<void> {
 32:       const key = `./components/mockups/${componentPath}.tsx`;
 33:       const loader = modules[key];
 34:       if (!loader) {
 35:         setError(`No component found at ${componentPath}.tsx`);
 36:         return;
 37:       }
 38:       try {
 39:         const mod = await loader();
 40:         if (cancelled) {
 41:           return;
 42:         }
 43:         const name = componentPath.split("/").pop()!;
 44:         const comp = _resolveComponent(mod, name);
 45:         if (!comp) {
 46:           setError(
 47:             `No exported React component found in ${componentPath}.tsx\n\nMake sure the file has at least one exported function component.`,
 48:           );
 49:           return;
 50:         }
 51:         setComponent(() => comp);
 52:       } catch (e) {
 53:         if (cancelled) {
 54:           return;
 55:         }
 56:         const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e);
 57:         setError(`Failed to load preview.\n${message}`);
 58:       }
 59:     }
 60:     void loadComponent();
 61:     return () => {
 62:       cancelled = true;
 63:     };
 64:   }, [componentPath, modules]);
 65:   if (error) {
 66:     return (
 67:       <pre style={{ color: "red", padding: "2rem", fontFamily: "system-ui" }}>
 68:         {error}
 69:       </pre>
 70:     );
 71:   }
 72:   if (!Component) return null;
 73:   return <Component />;
 74: }
 75: function getBasePath(): string {
 76:   return import.meta.env.BASE_URL.replace(/\/$/, "");
 77: }
 78: function getPreviewExamplePath(): string {
 79:   const basePath = getBasePath();
 80:   return `${basePath}/preview/ComponentName`;
 81: }
 82: function Gallery() {
 83:   return (
 84:     <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 flex items-center justify-center p-8">
 85:       <div className="text-center max-w-md">
 86:         <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-3">
 87:           Component Preview Server
 88:         </h1>
 89:         <p className="text-gray-500 mb-4">
 90:           This server renders individual components for the workspace canvas.
 91:         </p>
 92:         <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">
 93:           Access component previews at{" "}
 94:           <code className="bg-gray-100 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-gray-600">
 95:             {getPreviewExamplePath()}
 96:           </code>
 97:         </p>
 98:       </div>
 99:     </div>
100:   );
101: }
102: function getPreviewPath(): string | null {
103:   const basePath = getBasePath();
104:   const { pathname } = window.location;
105:   const local =
106:     basePath && pathname.startsWith(basePath)
107:       ? pathname.slice(basePath.length) || "/"
108:       : pathname;
109:   const match = local.match(/^\/preview\/(.+)$/);
110:   return match ? match[1] : null;
111: }
112: function App() {
113:   const previewPath = getPreviewPath();
114:   if (previewPath) {
115:     return (
116:       <PreviewRenderer
117:         componentPath={previewPath}
118:         modules={discoveredModules}
119:       />
120:     );
121:   }
122:   return <Gallery />;
123: }
124: export default App;

File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/mockup-sandbox/mockupPreviewPlugin.ts
================
  1: import { mkdirSync, writeFileSync } from "fs";
  2: import path from "path";
  3: import glob from "fast-glob";
  4: import chokidar from "chokidar";
  5: import type { FSWatcher } from "chokidar";
  6: import type { Plugin } from "vite";
  7: const MOCKUPS_DIR = "src/components/mockups";
  8: const GENERATED_MODULE = "src/.generated/mockup-components.ts";
  9: interface DiscoveredComponent {
 10:   globKey: string;
 11:   importPath: string;
 12: }
 13: export function mockupPreviewPlugin(): Plugin {
 14:   let root = "";
 15:   let currentSource = "";
 16:   let watcher: FSWatcher | null = null;
 17:   function getMockupsAbsDir(): string {
 18:     return path.join(root, MOCKUPS_DIR);
 19:   }
 20:   function getGeneratedModuleAbsPath(): string {
 21:     return path.join(root, GENERATED_MODULE);
 22:   }
 23:   function isMockupFile(absolutePath: string): boolean {
 24:     const rel = path.relative(getMockupsAbsDir(), absolutePath);
 25:     return (
 26:       !rel.startsWith("..") && !path.isAbsolute(rel) && rel.endsWith(".tsx")
 27:     );
 28:   }
 29:   function isPreviewTarget(relativeToMockups: string): boolean {
 30:     return relativeToMockups
 31:       .split(path.sep)
 32:       .every((segment) => !segment.startsWith("_"));
 33:   }
 34:   async function discoverComponents(): Promise<Array<DiscoveredComponent>> {
 35:     const files = await glob(`${MOCKUPS_DIR}/**/*.tsx`, {
 36:       cwd: root,
 37:       ignore: ["**/_*/**", "**/_*.tsx"],
 38:     });
 39:     return files.map((f) => ({
 40:       globKey: "./" + f.slice("src/".length),
 41:       importPath: path.posix.relative("src/.generated", f),
 42:     }));
 43:   }
 44:   function generateSource(components: Array<DiscoveredComponent>): string {
 45:     const entries = components
 46:       .map(
 47:         (c) =>
 48:           `  ${JSON.stringify(c.globKey)}: () => import(${JSON.stringify(c.importPath)})`,
 49:       )
 50:       .join(",\n");
 51:     return [
 52:       "// This file is auto-generated by mockupPreviewPlugin.ts.",
 53:       "type ModuleMap = Record<string, () => Promise<Record<string, unknown>>>;",
 54:       "export const modules: ModuleMap = {",
 55:       entries,
 56:       "};",
 57:       "",
 58:     ].join("\n");
 59:   }
 60:   function shouldAutoRescan(pathname: string): boolean {
 61:     return (
 62:       pathname.includes("/components/mockups/") ||
 63:       pathname.includes("/.generated/mockup-components")
 64:     );
 65:   }
 66:   let refreshInFlight = false;
 67:   let refreshQueued = false;
 68:   async function refresh(): Promise<boolean> {
 69:     if (refreshInFlight) {
 70:       refreshQueued = true;
 71:       return false;
 72:     }
 73:     refreshInFlight = true;
 74:     let changed = false;
 75:     try {
 76:       const components = await discoverComponents();
 77:       const newSource = generateSource(components);
 78:       if (newSource !== currentSource) {
 79:         currentSource = newSource;
 80:         const generatedModuleAbsPath = getGeneratedModuleAbsPath();
 81:         mkdirSync(path.dirname(generatedModuleAbsPath), { recursive: true });
 82:         writeFileSync(generatedModuleAbsPath, currentSource);
 83:         changed = true;
 84:       }
 85:     } finally {
 86:       refreshInFlight = false;
 87:     }
 88:     if (refreshQueued) {
 89:       refreshQueued = false;
 90:       const followUp = await refresh();
 91:       return changed || followUp;
 92:     }
 93:     return changed;
 94:   }
 95:   async function onFileAddedOrRemoved(): Promise<void> {
 96:     await refresh();
 97:   }
 98:   return {
 99:     name: "mockup-preview",
100:     enforce: "pre",
101:     configResolved(config) {
102:       root = config.root;
103:     },
104:     async buildStart() {
105:       await refresh();
106:     },
107:     async configureServer(viteServer) {
108:       await refresh();
109:       const mockupsAbsDir = getMockupsAbsDir();
110:       mkdirSync(mockupsAbsDir, { recursive: true });
111:       watcher = chokidar.watch(mockupsAbsDir, {
112:         ignoreInitial: true,
113:         awaitWriteFinish: {
114:           stabilityThreshold: 100,
115:           pollInterval: 50,
116:         },
117:       });
118:       watcher.on("add", (file) => {
119:         if (
120:           isMockupFile(file) &&
121:           isPreviewTarget(path.relative(mockupsAbsDir, file))
122:         ) {
123:           void onFileAddedOrRemoved();
124:         }
125:       });
126:       watcher.on("unlink", (file) => {
127:         if (isMockupFile(file)) {
128:           void onFileAddedOrRemoved();
129:         }
130:       });
131:       viteServer.middlewares.use((req, res, next) => {
132:         const requestUrl = new URL(req.url ?? "/", "http://127.0.0.1");
133:         const pathname = requestUrl.pathname;
134:         const originalEnd = res.end.bind(res);
135:         res.end = ((...args: Parameters<typeof originalEnd>) => {
136:           if (res.statusCode === 404 && shouldAutoRescan(pathname)) {
137:             void refresh();
138:           }
139:           return originalEnd(...args);
140:         }) as typeof res.end;
141:         next();
142:       });
143:     },
144:     async closeWatcher() {
145:       if (watcher) {
146:         await watcher.close();
147:       }
148:     },
149:   };
150: }

File: Visual-Brand-main/artifacts/website/public/info-loader.js
================
 1: (function () {
 2:   function applyInfo(info) {
 3:     document.querySelectorAll("[data-info]").forEach(function (el) {
 4:       var key = el.getAttribute("data-info");
 5:       var val = info[key];
 6:       if (val == null || val === "") return;
 7:       el.textContent = val;
 8:     });
 9:     document.querySelectorAll("[data-info-href]").forEach(function (el) {
10:       var spec = el.getAttribute("data-info-href");
11:       var parts = spec.split(":");
12:       var scheme = parts[0];
13:       var key = parts[1];
14:       var val = info[key];
15:       if (val == null || val === "") return;
16:       var href;
17:       if (scheme === "url") href = val;
18:       else if (scheme === "tel" || scheme === "sms") href = scheme + ":" + val;
19:       else if (scheme === "mailto") href = "mailto:" + val;
20:       else return;
21:       el.setAttribute("href", href);
22:     });
23:   }
24:   fetch("/api/business-info", { headers: { Accept: "application/json" } })
25:     .then(function (r) { return r.ok ? r.json() : null; })
26:     .then(function (info) { if (info) applyInfo(info); })
27:     .catch(function () {  });
28: })();

 94:       <p style="font-size:12px; color:var(--sand); margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:40px;">Flex blocks never expire. $1,200 flat rate is reserved for studio and 1-bedroom moves only. Larger homes scope as projects.</p>
 95:       <div style="background:var(--warm); border:1px solid var(--linen); padding:32px; margin-bottom:40px;">
 96:         <div style="font-size:12px; font-weight:700; letter-spacing:0.12em; text-transform:uppercase; color:var(--rust); margin-bottom:12px;">A Note on Labels</div>
 97:         <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8;">Labels are always included — handwritten on-site by default, and printed sets provided for larger project scopes. For efficiency, printed labels are usually handled as office work rather than billed hourly. I notate during the session, build the label set in my own app on my own time, print them, and bring them back to apply. This saves real money on hourly time that would otherwise be spent typing and cutting labels mid-session.</p>

House Calls fills the missing person role in real life: the partner who handled it, the nearby parent, the neighbor, the adult child in another city, the friend who always knew how to make the day still work.</p>

The appliance install that feels different when you're home alone. The digital login that somehow became intimidating overnight. The package, pickup, repair, donation, or appointment that shouldn't be a big deal but suddenly feels heavier than it should.</p>
 87:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--char); font-weight:600; margin-bottom:16px;">House Calls exists for the private, practical things people don't always want to say out loud.</p>
 88:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin-bottom:24px;">The goal is not to make life look perfect. The goal is to make everyday life feel safe, manageable, and less isolating when the normal support system changed.</p>

 42:   <a href="home-organization.html">Home Organization & Modern Move</a>
 43:   <a href="legacy.html">Legacy Planning & Inventory Catalog</a>

 49: <div class="page">
 50:   <section style="padding:80px 0 56px; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">
 51:     <div class="container" style="max-width:760px;">
 52:       <div class="label">02 — Legacy Planning & Inventory Catalog</div>
 53:       <h1 style="font-size:clamp(28px,4vw,48px); font-weight:700; color:var(--char); line-height:1.15; letter-spacing:-0.02em; margin-bottom:16px;">Clarity without fear.</h1>
 54:       <p style="font-size:17px; color:var(--stone); line-height:1.75; max-width:600px;">The operational side of a home, made visible again.</p>
 55:     </div>
 56:   </section>
 57:   <section style="padding:64px 0;">
 58:     <div class="container" style="max-width:760px;">
 59:       <div style="font-size:15px; line-height:1.9; color:var(--ink); margin-bottom:32px;">
 60:         <p style="margin-bottom:16px;">This is for the part of life most people don't realize has been quietly building for years — the things inside a home that became part of how life worked, long before anyone stopped to look at them.</p>
 61:         <p style="margin-bottom:8px; font-weight:600;">It is not estate planning.</p>
 62:         <p style="margin-bottom:8px; font-weight:600;">It is not asset planning.</p>
 63:         <p style="margin-bottom:8px; font-weight:600;">It is planning the actual pieces of a life.</p>
 64:         <p>Not the will, not the paperwork, not the part a lawyer handles. The part that lives inside the walls.</p>
 65:       </div>
 66:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:40px 0 16px;">Who this is for</h2>
 67:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--stone); margin-bottom:16px; line-height:1.75;">The operational side of a home shows up for almost everyone, eventually. Sometimes it's a life change. Sometimes it's a move. Sometimes it's a quiet morning where the drawers, closets, and storage spaces stop matching the person living there.</p>
 68:       <ul style="list-style:none; margin-bottom:24px;">
 69:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:10px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The divorced mom who moved into a condo and suddenly had to see, for the first time, how much had actually been accumulated over a marriage — and had to agree to how it all gets split</li>
 70:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:10px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The person who lived in the same apartment for ten years and had no idea how much had quietly gathered in the back of every closet</li>
 71:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:10px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The career change that revealed a hundred film industry cords, gear, and references in the garage — from a life that isn't the current one anymore</li>
 72:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:10px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The household where someone is ready to take control of their own story before it falls into someone else's hands</li>
 73:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:10px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The family carrying years of meaningful, valuable, or hard-to-sort volume that deserves clarity without pressure</li>
 74:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:10px 0;">The person who wants to decide what stays, what moves on, and what gets remembered — while they are the one making the decisions</li>
 75:       </ul>
 76:       <div style="background:var(--warm); border-left:3px solid var(--rust); padding:24px 28px; margin:40px 0;">
 77:         <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.9; margin-bottom:16px;">It's a holiday dinner, looking at china that hasn't been used in years. You wonder if it ever will, knowing three plates are missing, broken in memorable moments over lifetimes. What happens to a set of china passed down two generations, incomplete but once made a new couple feel whole? It can't be worthless, but can't be sold incomplete. Your kids live in small apartments and said, "That's sweet, but we can't take it." So, what happens to something you thought would be with your family forever?</p>
 78:         <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.9;">I help. I look at everything in your home — practical, sentimental, and holding memories — and I listen to them, for as long or as little as you want to tell their stories. We'll find a way to ensure the things you felt were special — incomplete and all — make it to hands that collect, treasure, and find value in them, sharing in the story a little longer.</p>
 79:       </div>
 80:       <p style="font-size:16px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:32px 0; font-style:italic;">This service is the person who can see what is actually there.</p>
 81:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:40px 0 16px;">What this work actually is</h2>
 82:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--stone); margin-bottom:16px;">The operational side of a home is the layer that quietly adds up over time:</p>
 83:       <ul style="list-style:none; margin-bottom:24px;">
 84:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The drawers</li>
 85:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The backup bedding</li>
 86:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The linen closets stacked with care</li>
 87:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The vintage pieces with story</li>
 88:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The everyday things with future value</li>
 89:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The candles tucked away because the house was always tidy enough</li>
 90:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">The designer pieces in sizes the family doesn't share</li>
 91:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0;">The objects that deserve clarity before family stress builds</li>
 92:       </ul>
 93:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin-bottom:40px;">Sometimes the people who love you don't share your eye, your size, or the history behind what you chose. That is not a failure of family. It is just the reality of inherited space — people can only hold what they recognize.</p>
 94:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 16px;">Possible outputs include</h2>
 95:       <div class="outputs-grid">
 96:         <span class="outputs-header">Possible outputs include</span>
 97:         <span>Digital inventory</span><span>Photo documentation</span>
 98:         <span>Room-by-room item notes</span><span>Family distribution references</span>
 99:         <span>Sentiment and story preservation</span><span>Resale-ready routing notes</span>
100:         <span>Donation pathways</span><span>Second-home and storage references</span>
101:         <span>Transition roadmap</span><span>Printable copies</span>
102:         <span>Bound family binders</span><span>Duplicate family copies</span>
103:         <span style="border-right:none;">Digital or web-based workflows</span><span></span>
104:       </div>
105:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin:32px 0;">When a piece has a story worth keeping with it, that history is documented too. That is the quiet bridge between Legacy Planning and Curated Resale. Items identified for sale during catalog work can route directly into Curated Resale & Consignment without restarting the process — and when story matters, the story travels with them.</p>
106:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:40px 0 16px;">How project timelines work</h2>
107:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin-bottom:40px;">Larger projects are completed across focused work sessions over a shared timeline, rather than continuous daily presence. A two-week catalog may look like three focused 11–4 sessions, with off-site documentation, resale routing, and continuity work completed between visits.</p>
108:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 20px;">Pricing</h2>

 49: <div class="page">
 50:   <section style="padding:80px 0 56px; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">
 51:     <div class="container" style="max-width:760px;">
 52:       <div class="label">04 — Curated Resale & Consignment</div>
 53:       <h1 style="font-size:clamp(28px,4vw,48px); font-weight:700; color:var(--char); line-height:1.15; letter-spacing:-0.02em; margin-bottom:16px;">Is it cool? Is it sellable? Will they even take it?</h1>
 54:       <p style="font-size:17px; color:var(--stone); line-height:1.75; max-width:600px;">Piece-by-piece curation from someone who knows the platforms. For the things that still have value, story, or second-market potential — without asking you to become a part-time reseller.</p>
 55:     </div>
 56:   </section>
 57:   <section style="padding:64px 0;">
 58:     <div class="container" style="max-width:760px;">
 59:       <div style="font-size:15px; line-height:1.9; color:var(--ink); margin-bottom:24px;">
 60:         <p style="margin-bottom:16px;">This service is best for items that have been well cared for, still hold real market interest, or deserve thoughtful placement through story-led resale.</p>
 61:         <p>It is not a donation pickup substitute, bulk textile recycling service, or a shortcut for things that are no longer in resellable condition.</p>
 62:       </div>
 63:       <div style="background:var(--warm); border:1px solid var(--linen); padding:28px; margin-bottom:40px;">
 64:         <div style="font-size:11px; font-weight:700; letter-spacing:0.12em; text-transform:uppercase; color:var(--rust); margin-bottom:8px;">Shop the closet</div>
 65:         <div style="font-size:15px; font-weight:600; color:var(--char); margin-bottom:6px;">The Well Lived Closet</div>
 66:         <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.7; margin-bottom:14px;">Curated pieces with a life left in them — designer, vintage, and the occasional treasure. Photographed clean. Shipped in two days.</p>
 67:         <div class="shop-buttons">
 68:           <a href="https://posh.mk/HLUmmsrzq2b" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Shop Poshmark →</a>
 69:           <a href="https://ebay.us/m/cUjlUb" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="alt">Shop eBay →</a>
 70:           <a href="https://instagram.com/thewelllivedcloset" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="alt">Follow the Closet on Instagram →</a>
 71:         </div>
 72:       </div>
 73:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 16px;">The work is not just listing. It includes:</h2>
 74:       <ul style="list-style:none; margin-bottom:40px;">
 75:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Pickup, intake, evaluation</li>
 76:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Photography</li>
 77:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Platform matching</li>
 78:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Buyer communication</li>
 79:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Routing and return logic</li>
 80:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Donation reroute when appropriate</li>
 81:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0;">Monthly reporting and payout rhythm</li>
 82:       </ul>
 83:       <p style="font-size:15px; font-weight:600; color:var(--char); margin-bottom:40px; font-style:italic;">The goal is to move the item into the right next life, not just the fastest sale.</p>
 84:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 16px;">Easy handoff and pickup</h2>
 85:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--stone); margin-bottom:16px;">The handoff is intentionally easy. Depending on what makes the most sense for your week, items can move through:</p>
 86:       <ul style="list-style:none; margin-bottom:16px;">
 87:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">City pickup</li>
 88:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Route-based stop-ins</li>
 89:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Uber Business courier</li>
 90:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Building desk drop</li>
 91:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">UPS Access Point</li>
 92:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0;">Direct bag shipment or handoff during another project block</li>
 93:       </ul>
 94:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--stone); margin-bottom:40px;">The philosophy is simple: why spend time coordinating a bag when it can be in my workflow and assessed for value by noon?</p>
 95:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 16px;">Item standards</h2>
 96:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin-bottom:16px;">This is a resale and curation service. It is not waste removal, donation hauling, contaminated textile removal, a recycling substitute, or a "please get rid of this for me" service.</p>
 97:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin-bottom:40px;">The assumption is: these are things you took care of and know deserve another life. That is the spirit of this service.</p>
 98:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 16px;">Where items sell</h2>
 99:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--stone); margin-bottom:16px;">Items are routed by category and market fit for maximum return:</p>
100:       <ul style="list-style:none; margin-bottom:16px;">
101:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Poshmark (Poshmark Ambassador)</li>
102:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">eBay</li>
103:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Etsy</li>
104:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Facebook Marketplace</li>
105:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Chairish</li>
106:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--linen);">Vinted, Vestiaire, Grailed</li>
107:         <li style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); padding:8px 0;">Vetted local high-end resale and private collector network</li>
108:       </ul>
109:       <p style="font-size:13px; color:var(--stone); margin-bottom:40px;">The route depends on item type, buyer demand, story value, platform behavior, seasonality, and speed versus premium price goals.</p>
110:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 16px;">Realistic resale timeline</h2>
111:       <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--ink); line-height:1.8; margin-bottom:40px;">This is a long game, not a fast-cash service. Most strong items sell within the first 90 days. Nearly everything with real demand finds its buyer within 6 to 9 months. The right expectation is: resale rewards patience, not urgency. If immediate cash is the priority, resale may not be the best route.</p>
112:       <h2 style="font-size:18px; font-weight:700; color:var(--char); margin:0 0 20px;">Commission structure</h2>
113:       <table class="pricing-table">
114:         <tr><td>Clothing & Accessories</td><td>55% Dayna / 45% client</td></tr>
115:         <tr><td>Designer</td><td>50 / 50</td></tr>
116:         <tr><td>Furniture & Significant Home Pieces</td><td>50 / 50</td></tr>
117:         <tr><td>Full Closet Liquidation</td><td>55 / 45</td></tr>
118:       </table>
119:       <p style="font-size:13px; color:var(--stone); margin-top:16px; line-height:1.6;">Monthly report by the 1st · Payout by the 5th · Clean split of net proceeds after platform fees</p>
120:       <p style="font-size:12px; color:var(--sand); margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:40px;">Agreement required. No upfront cost. Commission calculated on net proceeds after platform fees.</p>

 50:   <section style="padding: 80px 0 56px; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--linen);">
 51:     <div class="container" style="max-width: 760px;">
 52:       <div class="label">Meet Dayna</div>
 53:       <h1 style="font-size:clamp(28px,4vw,48px); font-weight:700; color:var(--char); line-height:1.15; letter-spacing:-0.02em; margin-bottom:0;">
 54:         competence does not eliminate the need to be cared for.
 55:       </h1>
 56:     </div>
 57:   </section>
 58:   <section style="padding: 64px 0;">
 59:     <div class="container" style="max-width: 760px;">
 60:       <div class="about-grid">
 61:         <div>
 62:           <div class="about-bio-copy" style="font-size:15px; line-height:1.9; color:var(--ink);">
 63:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">I have always been drawn to the life that lives inside people's most treasured possessions — the objects around which identity is formed, whether subtly or boldly.</p>
 64:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">A jacket is never just clothing when it carries the memory of the woman who wore it and the nights she spent wrapped in it beside the love of her life.</p>
 65:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">A record is never just vinyl when it still holds the rebellion, risk, and moment that brought it into the world — an era in which music helped bring authority to its knees.</p>
 66:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">A closed closet door is never just storage when it still tells the story of a marriage, a career, a season of confidence, or the person someone once was.</p>
 67:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">That instinct has followed me my entire life.</p>
 68:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">Creating the time, space, and experience for people to discover the belongings that will become part of their own story has always felt deeply important to me.</p>
 69:             <p style="margin-bottom:32px; font-size:17px; font-weight:600; color:var(--char); font-style:italic;">That is the heart of this work.</p>
 70:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">I do not believe people simply need help getting rid of things. I believe they need help understanding what those things mean, what they are worth, what they still have left to do, and where the next chapter of those belongings belongs.</p>
 71:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">Sometimes that means preserving. Sometimes it means cataloging, resale, or making sure a family story does not disappear into a donation pile.</p>
 72:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">The work is never really about the object. It is about protecting the life it represents.</p>
 73:             <hr class="divider" style="margin: 40px 0;"/>
 74:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">I came to understand the full weight of that truth in an entirely different way over the last year. After an unforeseen flood, I found myself moving through 13 temporary homes and Airbnbs, carrying only fragments of the life I thought I would always recognize.</p>
 75:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">Years of belongings, valuables, and deeply personal objects were damaged or lost — many of them irreplaceable.</p>
 76:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">What surprised me most was not only the grief of the loss itself, but the disorientation of living without the things that quietly reflect you back to yourself each day.</p>
 77:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">When it was my life, my loss, my dog beside me in a storage unit, and no clear sense yet of what the next version of home would be, I came face to face with something essential.</p>
 78:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">During that season, I was introduced to someone who, on paper, might have simply been called a home organizer. But what she offered was something far deeper. She stepped into the moments I could not hold alone. The decisions I was too depleted to make. The logistics I normally would have solved in seconds.</p>
 79:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px; font-size:17px; font-weight:600; color:var(--char);">She was not organizing. She was relief.</p>
 80:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">That experience changed the way I understand this work. Because when it is your own life in pieces, even the most capable person can lose access to their usual clarity. And in those moments, what matters most is not simply having someone who knows where things go. It is having someone who can step into the emotional and operational weight of transition and quietly help carry it with you.</p>
 81:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">I do not see homes as projects. I see them as living systems shaped by identity, family, safety, and transition.</p>
 82:             <p style="margin-bottom:20px;">My role is to step into complexity with calm, create clarity around belongings, preserve what matters, recover hidden value, and build elegant systems that help people move forward without losing the story of how they got here.</p>
 83:             <p style="margin-bottom:32px; font-size:16px; font-weight:600; color:var(--char);">At the core, I believe the most meaningful work is helping people feel truly taken care of. That is what this business was built to do.</p>
 84:             <a href="./contact.html" class="btn btn-dark">Get in Touch</a>
 85:           </div>
 86:         </div>

 97:             <div class="label about-background-label">Background</div>
 98:             <p>For more than 15 years, I have built my career creating environments that help people function beautifully in real life. I have led large-scale operations, teams, and transformation initiatives for national brands, designing systems that solve invisible friction before it becomes visible failure.</p>
 99:             <p>That same philosophy now lives inside The Well Lived Citizen.</p>
100:             <p>I bring together executive-level operational thinking, emotional discernment, resale and recoverable-value expertise, and a deep reverence for story, memory, and belonging.</p>

 73:     </details>

 76: <script>
 77: const form = document.getElementById('form');
 78: const status = document.getElementById('status');
 79: const pw = document.getElementById('pw');
 80: const jsonEl = document.getElementById('json');
 81: const loadBtn = document.getElementById('loadBtn');
 82: const saveBtn = document.getElementById('saveBtn');
 83: function setStatus(msg, kind) {
 84:   status.textContent = msg;
 85:   status.className = 'status' + (kind ? ' ' + kind : '');
 86: }
 87: async function load() {
 88:   setStatus('Loading...');
 89:   try {
 90:     const r = await fetch('/api/business-info');
 91:     if (!r.ok) throw new Error('HTTP ' + r.status);
 92:     const data = await r.json();
 93:     Object.entries(data).forEach(([k, v]) => {
 94:       const el = form.elements[k];
 95:       if (el) el.value = v ?? '';
 96:     });
 97:     jsonEl.textContent = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);
 98:     setStatus('Loaded.', 'ok');
 99:   } catch (e) {
100:     setStatus('Could not load: ' + e.message, 'err');
101:   }
102: }
103: form.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
104:   e.preventDefault();
105:   if (!pw.value) { setStatus('Enter the admin password first.', 'err'); return; }
106:   saveBtn.disabled = true;
107:   setStatus('Saving...');
108:   const data = {};
109:   Array.from(form.elements).forEach((el) => {
110:     if (el.name) data[el.name] = el.value;
111:   });
112:   try {
113:     const r = await fetch('/api/business-info', {
114:       method: 'PUT',
115:       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-admin-password': pw.value },
116:       body: JSON.stringify(data),
117:     });
118:     const body = await r.json().catch(() => ({}));
119:     if (!r.ok) throw new Error(body.error || ('HTTP ' + r.status));
120:     jsonEl.textContent = JSON.stringify(body, null, 2);
121:     setStatus('Saved. Reload any public page to see updates.', 'ok');
122:   } catch (e) {
123:     setStatus('Save failed: ' + e.message, 'err');
124:   } finally {
125:     saveBtn.disabled = false;
126:   }
127: });
128: loadBtn.addEventListener('click', load);
129: load();
130: </script>
131: </body>
132: </html>
